Xiamen was very cold on the day of check-in. The heating did not work after staying in the north room for two hours. I was shivering in the hotel room wearing a down jacket and several layers of clothes. I called the housekeeping depar**ent and they said the heating was good and I had to wait a little longer. The tone was official and indifferent. I called again an hour later to explain the situation. They said they would send the engineering depar**ent to check it out. After waiting for half an hour, no one came. I called the housekeeping depar**ent again. Fortunately, Zhang Liming answered the phone and immediately arranged for the engineering depar**ent to come to the door for inspection. She also went to the room to confirm it herself. Together, we determined that the air outlet temperature was enough but the wind was insufficient. We immediately arranged to change the room on the south side and assisted me in moving things to change rooms. When I arrived at the opposite room, it was already heated up only 5 minutes before the engineer left. At that time, I was very grateful for Miss Zhang's service and promised to write down her name to comment and praise her. Afterwards, I was too busy to delay until now. Today, I looked through my bag and saw this card left to remind myself to comment at that time and came to praise her quickly. I hope that other staff in your hotel can have the attitude and ability to solve problems like Miss Zhang. Problems are not solved by delaying. Only by responding to guests' needs quickly can problems be solved. Thank you.
